### [1] [Geometric Rigidity via Harmonic Twisted Spinors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19567)
*Francesco Bei,Simone Cecchini*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文利用Gromov精确闭2-形式的提升方法，在闭自旋流形上证明了标量曲率与万有覆盖谱底之间的尖锐双曲比较，并通过调和旋量构造了Einstein度量及实双曲万有覆盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Gromov的精确闭2-形式提升方法系统引入标量曲率几何，建立标量曲率与万有覆盖拉普拉斯谱底之间的最优比较，并刻画等号成立时的刚性几何结构。

Method: 利用Gromov扭曲L²-指标定理，通过一族小酉扭曲产生调和旋量；在等号情形，通过精细Kato等式缺陷的共形解释，利用调和旋量构造关于共形度量下的平行旋量，从而证明原度量是Einstein的；在正谱情形进一步证明万有覆盖为实双曲空间。

Result: 证明了闭自旋流形上标量曲率与万有覆盖谱底之间的尖锐双曲比较不等式；刻画了等号成立条件：原度量Einstein，且在正谱情形万有覆盖为实双曲空间。

Conclusion: Gromov精确2-形式提升方法为标量曲率几何提供了新的工具，建立了拓扑（同调非平凡闭2-形式）、分析（谱底）与几何（双曲/Einstein结构）之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We study Gromov's exact-lift two-form method in scalar-curvature geometry. For a closed Riemannian spin manifold carrying a homologically non-trivial closed two-form whose lift to the universal cover is exact, we prove the sharp hyperbolic scalar-curvature comparison with the bottom of the spectrum of the universal Riemannian covering. The two-form enters through Gromov's twisted \(L^2\)-index, which produces harmonic spinors for a family of small unitary twists. We analyze the equality case by interpreting the refined Kato equality defect conformally and use the harmonic spinors to construct a parallel spinor with respect to a suitable conformally related metric. This yields that the original metric is Einstein. In the positive-spectrum case, this method implies that the universal cover is real hyperbolic.

</details>


### [2] [Some constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature metrics on open manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19619)
*Anushree Das*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文构造了开流形上一致正标量曲率的完备黎曼度量。对于n≥3维，若流形存在有界下方且无≥n-2指数临界点的适当Morse函数，或存在具有紧穷举且每个边界为极小的正标量曲率度量，则可得一致正标量曲率度量。对于4≤n≤7维，若流形具有乘积端和C-二次衰减（C>4π²）的正标量曲率度量，则远离基点的平均凸超曲面可导出一致正标量曲率度量。作为应用，若开流形无一致正标量曲率度量但有平均凸穷举，则其端部存在平均凸叶状结构；若有平均凹穷举，则端部存在平均凹叶状结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在微分几何中，一致正标量曲率度量（具有正下界的标量曲率）比通常的正标量曲率更强，其存在性条件更为苛刻。本文试图在开流形（非紧完备流形）上建立多种构造方法，探索不同拓扑与几何条件下该度量的存在性判据。

Method: （1）利用Morse理论：通过适当Morse函数的临界点指数条件（无≥n-2指数临界点）构造度量；（2）极小边界条件：利用紧穷举中每个边界为极小的正标量曲率度量进行构造；（3）乘积端与二次衰减：结合C-二次衰减（C>4π²）条件和平均凸超曲面的存在性，在4≤n≤7维下构造；（4）应用方面：通过穷举性质推导端部的叶状结构。

Result: （1）n≥3时，存在无≥n-2指数临界点的Morse函数⇒存在一致正标量曲率度量；（2）n≥3时，存在正标量曲率度量+极小边界穷举⇒存在一致正标量曲率度量；（3）4≤n≤7时，存在正标量曲率度量（C-二次衰减，C>4π²）+远离基点的平均凸超曲面⇒存在一致正标量曲率度量；（4）无一致正标量曲率但有平均凸穷举⇒端部有平均凸叶状结构；有平均凹穷举⇒端部有平均凹叶状结构。

Conclusion: 本文系统建立了一致正标量曲率度量在开流形上的多种构造机制，揭示了Morse函数临界点指数、边界几何（极小/平均凸/平均凹）以及度量衰减率之间的深层联系，为理解开流形上标量曲率的几何约束提供了新工具。

Abstract: We obtain several constructions of uniformly positive scalar curvature complete Riemannian metrics on open manifolds. For dimension $n\geq3$, we show that if such a manifold admits a proper Morse function $f$ bounded below such that $f$ has no critical points of index $\geq n-2$, then it admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. On the other hand if such a manifold admits a positive scalar curvature metric along with a compact exhaustion $\{U_i\}$ such that the boundary of each $U_i$ is minimal, then it also admits a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric. For dimension $4 \leq n\leq 7$, we show that if the manifold has product ends and a positive scalar curvature metric with $C$-quadratic decay at infinity for $C>4π^2$ with respect to some basepoint, then the existence of a mean convex hypersurface far enough from the basepoint implies the existence of a uniformly positive scalar curvature metric on the manifold. We study some applications of these results, including showing that if an open manifold of dimension $n\geq 3$ that admits no uniformly positive scalar curvature metric has a positive scalar curvature metric with mean convex exhaustion, then it admits a mean convex foliation of compact sets sufficiently close to the ends. On the other hand, if such a manifold has a mean concave exhaustion, then its ends admit a mean concave foliation.

</details>


### [3] [Positive mass theorem and the Yamabe equation on CR manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19801)
*Jih-Hsin Cheng*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文综述了CR流形上正质量定理和Yamabe方程的最新进展，重点介绍了[CMY17]、[CMY23]和[CC22]三项工作，分别涉及三维CR几何中的正质量定理、Rossi球的CR-Sobolev商以及五维情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统梳理CR几何中正质量定理与Yamabe问题的研究进展，总结该领域的核心成果与发展脉络。

Method: 引入多复变或CR几何中的质量概念，通过CR-Sobolev商的极小化问题研究CR流形上的Yamabe问题，并利用正质量定理处理正曲率情形下的最小能量解。

Result: 正质量定理在求解正曲率情形下具有最小能量的Yamabe方程中起关键作用；团队在三维CR几何正质量定理、Rossi球CR-Sobolev商、五维情形分别取得重要进展。

Conclusion: 正质量定理是CR流形上Yamabe问题求解的核心工具，团队在三维和五维情形下的工作为该领域提供了重要理论支撑。

Abstract: Our goal is to survey the development of positive mass theorem and the Yamabe equation on CR manifolds in recent years. We introduce the notion of the mass in several complex variables or CR geometry. We then consider the Yamabe problem on CR manifolds to find a minimizer for the CR-Sobolev quotient. The positive mass theorem plays a key role in finding a solution to the Yamabe equation with minimum energy for the positive curvature case. We mainly focus on the team works in the following three papers [CMY17], [CMY23] and [CC22], on a positive mass theorem in 3-dimensional CR geometry, the CR-Sobolev quotient of Rossi spheres, and the 5-dimensional situation, respectively.

</details>


### [4] [The top Yau--Yang conjecture for Kähler manifolds with positive sectional curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19806)
*Ved V. Datar,Vamsi P. Pingali,Harish Seshadri*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了具有正截面曲率的完备非紧Kähler流形的Ricci形式的顶幂次具有有限积分，并利用Chen-Zhu的结果，在有界截面曲率假设下得到这类流形是拟射影的。证明中的关键新思想是使用带有限Monge-Ampère质量的Lipschitz权函数来证明Bézout估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有正截面曲率的完备非紧Kähler流形的几何性质，特别是其Ricci形式的积分性质，并探索这类流形的代数几何结构（拟射影性）。

Method: 使用带有限Monge-Ampère质量的Lipschitz权函数，结合Bézout估计，证明Ricci形式顶幂次的有限积分性质。

Result: 证明了完备非紧Kähler流形在正截面曲率条件下，其Ricci形式的顶幂次具有有限积分；结合Chen-Zhu的结果，在有界截面曲率假设下，这类流形是拟射影的。

Conclusion: 正截面曲率完备非紧Kähler流形的Ricci曲率顶幂次积分有限，且在截面曲率有界时流形为拟射影。

Abstract: We prove that the top wedge power of the Ricci form of a complete non-compact Kähler manifold with positive sectional curvature has finite integral. Using a result of Chen-Zhu, an immediate consequence is the quasiprojectivity of such manifolds under the assumption of bounded sectional curvature. A key new idea to prove Bézout estimates along with a Lipschitz weight with finite Monge-Ampère mass is used in the proof of the main result.

</details>


### [5] [Spectral Positive Mass Theorem for Asymptotically Hyperbolic 3-manifolds with Toroidal Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19858)
*Xiaoxiang Chai,Yimin Chen,Juncheol Pyo*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文针对具有环面无穷远的渐近双曲三维流形，定义了适应于谱标量曲率的质量不变量，并证明在谱标量曲率下界条件下该不变量的正性。此外，还证明了类似假设下的刚性定理和带宽估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将正质量定理和刚性结果推广到更一般的几何设定——具有环面无穷远的渐近双曲流形，并使用谱标量曲率（而非经典标量曲率）作为几何条件。

Method: 定义了一个新的质量不变量，该不变量适应于谱标量曲率；结合谱几何与双曲流形上的分析工具，在谱标量曲率下界条件下证明其正性，并导出刚性定理和带宽估计。

Result: 成功定义了适应谱标量曲率的质量不变量；证明了在谱标量曲率有下界时该不变量为正；得到了相应的刚性定理以及带宽估计。

Conclusion: 研究发展了渐近双曲流形的质量理论，将经典结果从标量曲率推广至谱标量曲率，并为相关几何与分析问题提供了新的工具和结果。

Abstract: We define a mass invariant adapted to the spectral scalar curvature for asymptotically hyperbolic 3-manifolds with toroidal infinity and show its positivity under a lower bound on the spectral scalar curvature. In addition, we show a rigidity theorem and some band width estimates under similar assumptions.

</details>


### [6] [Poisson and Jacobi structures from 2-covariant tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20030)
*Manuel de León,Xavier Gràcia,Rubén Izquierdo-López,Ángel Martínez-Muñoz,Xavier Rivas*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，通过研究非退化2-协变张量诱导的Poisson和Jacobi结构，推导了Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，该公式以某分布的曲率和微分形式的外微分给出了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍，并统一恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号，最后刻画了fat丛和p阶几乎余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Poisson和Jacobi结构在经典力学的几何描述中具有基础性作用，但通常由非退化2-协变张量诱导的双向量场所对应的括号构造缺乏统一的框架。本文旨在建立这一统一框架，并推导Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，以刻画Poisson或Jacobi结构存在的障碍。

Method: 在张量满足适当假设的条件下，推导了与相伴双向量场相关的Schouten-Nijenhuis括号的计算公式，该公式涉及某分布的曲率项和微分形式的外微分项。

Result: 获得了Poisson或Jacobi结构存在性的障碍公式；统一恢复了辛、局部共形辛、余辛和接触几何中的经典括号；刻画了fat丛和p阶几乎余辛结构确定Jacobi括号的条件。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一框架有效地统一了几种重要的几何结构中的括号构造，并为判断给定张量能否诱导Poisson或Jacobi结构提供了可计算的判据。

Abstract: Poisson and Jacobi structures play a fundamental role in the geometric description of many systems arising in classical mechanics. In most cases, the corresponding bivector field is induced by a non-degenerate 2-covariant tensor. In this paper, we present a unified framework for constructing the associated brackets by studying the Poisson and Jacobi structures induced by these tensors. More specifically, under suitable assumptions on the tensor, we derive a formula for computing the Schouten-Nijenhuis bracket of the associated bivector field in terms of the curvature of a certain distribution and the exterior derivative of a differential form. This formula provides the obstruction to the existence of a Poisson or Jacobi structure. To illustrate the theory, we recover the classical brackets associated with symplectic, locally conformally symplectic, cosymplectic, and contact geometries. Finally, we characterize the conditions under which fat bundles and almost cosymplectic structures of order $p$ determine a Jacobi bracket.

</details>


### [7] [Comparison Theorems for the Profile Curve Equation of Rotationally Symmetric Self-Shrinkers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20276)
*Peng Peng*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文从常微分方程角度研究旋转对称自收缩子，通过分析垂直点轨迹族的相交性给出了Angenent环面存在性的新证明，并推导线性化方程，利用Sturm型比较定理获得水平点轨迹单调性的充分条件，为解决Angenent环面唯一性问题提供了可能路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Angenent环面是平均曲率流中最重要的紧致嵌入自收缩子之一，但其唯一性是一个长期未解决的重要开放问题。本文旨在为这一唯一性问题提供新的理论工具和研究途径。

Method: 将旋转对称自收缩子问题转化为常微分方程，分析轮廓曲线的垂直点及其轨迹；通过证明两族垂直点轨迹必须相交来给出Angenent环面存在性的新证明；推导线性化方程并应用Sturm型比较定理，研究水平点轨迹的单调性。

Result: 给出了Angenent环面存在性的新证明；推导了旋转对称自收缩子的线性化方程；得到了水平点轨迹单调性的充分条件；在球面自收缩子附近建立了比较定理，并获得了水平点曲线的部分单调性结果。

Conclusion: 本文为Angenent环面的唯一性问题提供了新的理论框架和可能的解决途径，但尚未完全解决该唯一性问题。

Abstract: Mean curvature flow is a fundamental geometric evolution equation in which a submanifold moves in the normal direction with velocity equal to its mean curvature vector. Self-shrinkers arise naturally as self-similar solutions to the mean curvature flow and play an important role as models for finite-time singularities. Among nontrivial examples of compact embedded self-shrinkers, the rotationally symmetric self-shrinking torus constructed by Angenent is one of the most important. However, the uniqueness of the Angenent torus remains a major open problem.
  In this paper, we study rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers of type $\mathbb{S}^{1}\times \mathbb{S}^{n-1}$ from the point of view of ordinary differential equations. We analyze the profile curves of rotationally symmetric self-shrinkers, focusing on the behavior of their vertical points and the curves traced out by these points as the initial height varies. We give a new proof of the existence of the Angenent torus by showing that two families of vertical-point trajectories must intersect.
  We further derive the linearized equation associated with the rotationally symmetric self-shrinker equation and apply a Sturm-type comparison theorem to obtain sufficient conditions for the monotonicity of horizontal-point trajectories. In particular, we prove a comparison theorem for solutions near the spherical self-shrinker $x^{2}+r^{2}=2n$, and establish partial monotonicity results for the curves of horizontal points. These results provide a possible approach to the uniqueness problem for the Angenent torus.

</details>


### [8] [The Hermitian-Yang-Mills Iteration on Stable Bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20307)
*Huai-Dong Cao,Xiaofeng Sun,Shing-Tung Yau,Yingying Zhang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文基于Fan-Wang-Yang-Yau关于预定Hermitian-Yang-Mills张量及其扭曲变体的最新结果，提出了稳定全纯向量丛上Hermitian-Einstein度量的动力学构造，并将其推广到Higgs丛。附录中利用热流方法给出了扭曲预定HYM张量方程及其Higgs丛推广的解的存在唯一性的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为稳定全纯向量丛上的Hermitian-Einstein度量提供一种动力学构造方法，并将该构造推广到Higgs丛，同时为扭曲预定HYM张量方程提供新的存在唯一性证明。

Method: 基于Fan-Wang-Yang-Yau关于预定HYM张量及其扭曲变体的最新结果，采用动力学构造方法（可能涉及热流或相关演化方程）；附录中使用热流法证明扭曲预定HYM张量方程解的存在唯一性。

Result: 成功给出了稳定全纯向量丛上Hermitian-Einstein度量的动力学构造，并将其拓展至Higgs丛；在附录中给出了扭曲预定HYM张量方程及其Higgs丛推广的解的存在唯一性新证明。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了Hermitian-Einstein度量的一种新的动力学构造框架，并推广到了Higgs丛情形，同时提供了扭曲预定HYM张量方程的另一种证明路径，丰富了该领域的理论工具。

Abstract: In this paper, based on recent results for the prescribed Hermitian-Yang-Mills (HYM) tensor and its twisted variants by Fan-Wang-Yang-Yau, we provide a dynamical construction of Hermitian-Einstein metrics on stable holomorphic vector bundles and its extension to Higgs bundles. Additionally, in the appendix, we use the heat flow method to give a new proof of the existence and uniqueness of solutions to the twisted prescribed HYM tensor equation, as well as its generalization to Higgs bundles.

</details>


### [9] [The alignment time function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20481)
*Marco van den Beld-Serrano*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究在稳定因果时空中，给定一个指向过去的类时向量场，是否存在一个时间函数使其梯度与该向量场最优对齐。通过引入一个捕捉两者之间未对齐程度并惩罚零梯度的泛函，证明了在适当条件下存在唯一的光滑时间函数（称为对齐时间函数），并建立了其陡峭性改进、稳定性及对称继承等性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论中，时间函数的选择具有重要的几何与物理意义。给定一个类时向量场（如观测者的四速度场），自然希望找到与之尽可能对齐的时间函数，以便更好地描述时空的因果结构和动力学。

Method: 构造了一个泛函，该泛函一方面度量类时向量场与Sobolev函数梯度之间的未对齐程度，另一方面对零梯度进行惩罚。在光滑稳定因果时空的紧致子集上，基于Sobolev指数和零梯度惩罚强度的适当假设，证明了存在唯一的最小化元，即光滑的时间函数。

Result: 证明了在适当条件下存在唯一的光滑对齐时间函数；该函数可以通过规范程序改善其陡峭性；在$C^p$收敛下对度量和向量场具有稳定性；并且继承了度量和给定向量场的对称性。

Conclusion: 对齐时间函数为给定类时向量场提供了最优协同的时间函数选择，其良好的性质确保了在几何分析和相对论应用中的实用性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Given a fixed past-directed timelike vector field, does there exist a time function whose gradient is optimally aligned with it? We address this question by introducing a functional that, on the one hand, captures the misalignment between the timelike vector field and the gradients of suitable Sobolev functions, and, on the other hand, penalizes null gradients. Our analysis focuses on compact subsets of smooth stably causal spacetimes. More precisely, we prove that, under suitable assumptions on the Sobolev index and the strength of the null gradient penalization, there exists a unique smooth temporal function which minimizes the considered functional. We refer to this minimizer as the \emph{alignment time function}. Furthermore, several useful properties of the alignment time function are established: there exists a canonical procedure to improve its steepness, it is stable under $C^{p}$ convergence of the underlying metrics and vector fields and it inherits the symmetries shared by the metric and the given vector field.

</details>


### [10] [Approximation and interactive design with exact 3D elastic curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20516)
*David Brander,Jens Gravesen,Marc Isern*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从任意空间曲线段到3D弹性曲线（elastica）的快速稳定逼近方法。通过11参数解析表示（等价于球摆方程），实现了弹性曲线段的重建与逼近，并应用于交互式设计和CAD曲面合理化（如机器人热刀切割）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹性空间曲线在弯曲能量最小化约束下具有重要几何意义，但缺乏从任意曲线高效恢复其弹性参数的方法。本文旨在提供一种数值稳定的参数恢复算法，以支持弹性曲线的交互设计及工业应用（如机器人切割路径优化）。

Method: 1. 将弹性曲线等价于球摆方程，建立11参数解析表示；2. 提出从给定弹性曲线段恢复11参数的数值稳定方法；3. 基于参数恢复，实现任意空间曲线段到3D弹性曲线的快速逼近。

Result: 实现了对任意空间曲线段的弹性曲线逼近，方法具有快速、数值稳定的特点。案例展示了在交互式弹性曲线设计和CAD曲面合理化（机器人热刀切割）中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文的11参数弹性曲线表示与恢复算法为弹性曲线的几何建模提供了实用工具，在交互设计及工业制造（如机器人切割）中具有应用价值。

Abstract: An elastic space curve is a critical point of the bending energy subject to appropriate constraints. An analytic representation, equivalent to the spherical pendulum equation, leads to an 11-parameter description of the space of 3D elastic curve segments. We give a numerically stable method for recovering the 11 parameters from a given elastic curve segment. Using this, we give a fast and stable method to approximate an arbitrary space curve segment by a 3D elastica. Applications include interactive design with exact elastic curves and CAD surface rationalization for robotic hot-blade cutting.

</details>


### [11] [Positive Scalar Curvature Obstructions via Singular Dimension Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20528)
*Yuchen Bi,Jintian Zhu*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文受近期共形爆破方法进展启发，发展了Schoen-Yau型奇异维度下降方法，用于任意维度的正数量曲率障碍研究。证明了可扩张流形上的正数量曲率障碍，建立了相应的立方宽度不等式和二维系统估计。该方法还适用于可扩张AM-PI空间，当奇异集的Assouad余维数大于3-2/n时给出正数量曲率障碍。

Method: 基于Schoen-Yau型奇异维度下降方法，结合共形爆破技术，构建适用于任意维度的分析方法，并扩展到AM-PI空间。

Result: 证明了可扩张流形上的正数量曲率障碍，建立了立方宽度不等式和二维系统估计；在AM-PI空间上，当奇异集Assouad余维数大于3-2/n时也得到正数量曲率障碍。

Conclusion: 所发展的奇异维度下降方法为研究正数量曲率障碍提供了新工具，拓展了经典Schoen-Yau理论到更一般的空间和奇异情形。

Abstract: In light of recent advances in conformal blow-up methods for the positive mass theorem, including He--Shi--Yu, Bi--Hao--He--Shi--Zhu, and Brendle--Wang, we develop a Schoen--Yau type singular dimension descent method for positive scalar curvature obstructions in arbitrary dimensions. We prove obstructions to positive scalar curvature on enlargeable manifolds and establish the corresponding cubical width inequalities and two-systole estimates. The method also applies to enlargeable AM--PI spaces, giving a positive scalar curvature obstruction when the singular set has Assouad codimension greater than \(3-2/n\).

### [12] [Universal Properties of Nonlinearly Perturbed Maxwell Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19845)
*Tengyang Liu,Yisong Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了一类广义非线性微扰麦克斯韦电磁理论具有三个普适基本性质：有限能量的点电荷、排除有限能量的磁单极和双荷子、以及点电荷有效半径的任意小性及其局域不可检测性，为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供了经典解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性微扰麦克斯韦理论是否能够同时保持有限能量点电荷、排除磁单极和双荷子、以及点电荷有效半径任意小这三个普适性质，并为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供经典层面的解释。

Method: 构建一个对麦克斯韦理论进行最小非线性微扰的理论框架，其非线性度尽可能一般化，同时确保上述三个普适性质得到保持。通过数学推导证明这些性质的普适性。

Result: 证明了该非线性理论确实同时具备三个普适性质：有限能量点电荷存在、磁单极和双荷子被排除、点电荷有效半径可任意小且局域不可检测。

Conclusion: 该非线性理论为电子作为点电荷的不可见性提供了经典解释，且其非线性微扰方式在保持三个普适性质的前提下达到了最大程度的普遍性。

Abstract: We show that a general nonlinearly perturbed Maxwell theory of electromagnetism possesses three universal fundamental properties:
  (i) A finite-energy electric point charge.
  (ii) Exclusion of finite-energy magnetic monopoles and dually charged dyons.
  (iii) Arbitrary smallness of the effective radius of a point electric charge and the associated local undetectedness of the electric charge and energy.
  In particular, this last property offers a classical explanation for the invisibility of the electron, as a point electric charge, in accordance with the smallness of its effective radius.
  This nonlinear theory of electromagnetism has the feature that it minimally perturbs the Maxwell theory with a nonlinearity profile that is as general as possible such that the three universal properties stated above are all maintained.

### [13] [Dirac structures on tangent bundles: a geometric framework for variational principles, constrained dynamics, and symmetry reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20012)
*Hiroaki Yoshimura*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种称为“拉格朗日-狄拉克结构”的几何框架，该结构由（可能退化的）拉格朗日量和约束分布自然诱导，统一描述了非完整系统、退化拉格朗日系统和对称系统等动力学系统，并发展了相应的变分原理、约化理论及无穷维推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有几何动力学框架（如拉格朗日-达朗贝尔方程、狄拉克结构）在处理非完整约束、退化拉格朗日系统及对称约化时缺乏统一的几何描述，尤其非完整动力学不保持拉格朗日二形式，需要更普适的几何结构来统一刻画这些系统的动力学行为。

Method: 在切丛上构造由拉格朗日二形式和约束分布诱导的拉格朗日-狄拉克结构；提出切丛上的内蕴变分原理（拉格朗日-达朗贝尔-狄拉克原理）；利用李群对称性发展约化理论，导出约化后的欧拉-庞加莱-狄拉克方程；通过具体例子（带电粒子、电路、速度线性拉格朗日系统）及无穷维推广（理想流体）验证理论框架。

Result: 建立了拉格朗日-狄拉克结构，它在超正则情形下恢复拉格朗日-达朗贝尔方程的一阶形式；证明了非完整动力学虽然不保持拉格朗日二形式，但该结构在规范变换下得以保持，具有规范协变性；发展了约化理论得到欧拉-庞加莱-狄拉克方程及相应的约化变分原理；成功将理论应用于带电粒子、电路、速度线性系统及理想流体。

Conclusion: 拉格朗日-狄拉克结构为约束动力学系统提供了一致且统一的几何框架，兼具规范协变性和可约化性，并能自然推广到无穷维系统，为后续连续介质力学和几何力学的研究奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: We introduce a Dirac structure on the tangent bundle of a configuration manifold, called a \textit{Lagrange--Dirac structure}, which is naturally induced by the Lagrangian two-form associated with a (possibly degenerate) Lagrangian and a constraint distribution. This structure provides a unified geometric framework for Lagrange--Dirac dynamical systems, encompassing nonholonomic, degenerate Lagrangian, and symmetric systems. In the hyperregular case, the system recovers a first-order formulation of the Lagrange--d'Alembert equations. Although nonholonomic dynamics does not preserve the Lagrangian two-form, we show that the underlying Lagrange--Dirac structure is preserved up to gauge transformations, yielding a natural gauge covariance property.
  We also formulate an intrinsic variational principle directly on the tangent bundle, referred to as the \textit{Lagrange--d'Alembert--Dirac principle}, which recovers Hamilton's principle in the unconstrained case and the Lagrange--d'Alembert principle in the hyperregular constrained case. Furthermore, we develop a reduction theory for systems with Lie group symmetry, deriving a reduced Lagrange--Dirac structure over the Lie algebra that yields the Euler--Poincaré--Dirac equations and a corresponding reduced variational principle. Finally, we illustrate the theory through examples including charged particles, electric circuits, and systems with Lagrangians linear in velocity, and present an infinite-dimensional extension to ideal fluids that naturally incorporates the incompressibility constraint and recovers the Euler equations.

</details>

Our primary focus is to establish precise estimates on the number of negative eigenvalues (bound states) induced by the attractive perturbation. These results offer new insights into how randomness enhances the eigenvalue bounds.

### [17] [A simple proof for Hochster's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20016)
*Stefan Schröer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文为Hochster定理给出了一个概念性证明，即每个谱空间都同胚于某个环的谱。通过将有限Kolmogoroff空间以函子方式附加到环上，构造了一个滤过直接极限环，简化了Ershov的论证。关键要素包括用余等子和推出将有限Kolmogoroff空间组装成一维空间，以及Schwede关于环的笛卡尔平方中素理想的观察。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 给定一个基域和一个谱空间，将环构造为素数有限环的滤过直接极限，这些环以函子方式附加到有限Kolmogoroff空间上。关键步骤是利用余等子和推出将有限Kolmogoroff空间组装成一维空间，并结合Schwede关于环的笛卡尔平方中素理想的观察。

Result: 成功为Hochster定理给出了一个概念性证明，该证明简化了Ershov的论证，并且构造是函子性的。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个更简洁、概念化的Hochster定理证明，其构造方法具有函子性，为进一步研究谱空间与环谱之间的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: We give a conceptual proof for Hochster's Theorem, which asserts that each spectral space is homeomorphic to the spectrum of a ring. Given a ground field and a spectral space, our ring is constructed as filtered direct limit of prime-finite ring, which are attached in a functorial way to finite Kolmogoroff spaces. The construction simplifies an argument of Ershov along these lines. Our crucial ingredient is an assembly of finite Kolmogoroff spaces in terms of coequalizers and pushouts of one-dimensional spaces, and Schwede's observation on prime ideals in cartesian squares of rings.

### [19] [Wild automorphisms and compound isotriviality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20228)
*Jason Bell,Rahim Moosa*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文引入了“复合基本等平凡”自同构类（代数动力系统），证明每个野性自同构的阿贝尔簇都属于此类，且反之亦然——即射影不可约簇上若存在复合基本等平凡的野性自同构，则该簇必为阿贝尔簇。这证明了Reichstein–Rogalski–Zhang野性自同构猜想在复合基本等平凡动力系统中的情形，并给出了该猜想到非自治σ-簇情形的反例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受特征零差分域模型论的启发，旨在系统刻画代数簇上“野性”（wild）自同构的结构，并证明Reichstein–Rogalski–Zhang提出的野性自同构猜想在特定动力系统类中的成立性。

Method: 通过有限序列的等变纤维化，将（可能非自治的）代数动力系统经过基扩张后平凡化，构造复合基本等平凡动力系统；利用阿贝尔簇上自同构的结构性质进行分类论证。

Result: 阿贝尔簇上的每个野性自同构都是复合基本等平凡的；反之，任何不可约射影簇若具有复合基本等平凡的野性自同构，则其必为阿贝尔簇。此外，给出了该猜想到非自治σ-簇情形的反例。

Conclusion: 在复合基本等平凡动力系统的框架下，野性自同构猜想成立，且阿贝尔簇是唯一承载此类动力系统的不可约射影簇；同时指出猜想的非自治推广并不成立。

Abstract: Inspired by the model theory of difference fields in characteristic zero, a class of automorphisms of an algebraic variety, here called compound fundamental isotrivial, is introduced. These are algebraic dynamical systems that are built up via a finite sequence of equivariant fibrations from (possibly nonautonomous) algebraic dynamics which trivialise after base extension over themselves. Every wild automorphism of an abelian variety is compound fundamental isotrivial. Conversely, it is shown that the only irreducible projective varieties admitting a wild automorphism that is compound fundamental isotrivial are the abelian varieties. That is, the wild automorphism conjecture of Reichstein, Rogalski, and Zhang is here proven for compound fundamental isotrivial dynamics. Along the way, a counterexample to the naive generalisation of the conjecture to the nonautonomous setting of $σ$-varieties is provided.

### [20] [Anti-Zariski pairs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20268)
*Peng Ren,Eugenii Shustin*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出了"反Zariski对"的新概念，即两条复平面代数曲线$C',C''\subset\PP^2$，使得$(\PP^2,C')$与$(\PP^2,C'')$同胚，但$C'$与$C''$属于等奇异族的不同分支，并给出了具体例子及相关讨论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Zariski于1929年发现存在相同次数且具有相同奇异点集合的两条复平面代数曲线，但它们在平面中的嵌入方式拓扑不同，即属于等奇异族的不同分支。该现象至今被广泛研究。本文试图从相反视角出发，探讨是否存在拓扑相同（$(\PP^2,C')$与$(\PP^2,C'')$同胚）但等奇异族分支不同的曲线对，即"反Zariski对"。

Method: 通过理论分析，提出"反Zariski对"的定义，并构造具体例子予以展示，同时讨论相关性质与问题。

Result: 成功构造了反Zariski对的例子，表明存在$(\PP^2,C')$与$(\PP^2,C'')$同胚但分属不同等奇异族分支的曲线对。

Conclusion: 反Zariski对的存在性被证实，这为理解代数曲线嵌入拓扑与等奇异族结构之间的关系提供了新的视角，丰富了该领域的研究。

Abstract: In 1929, O. Zariski found a pair of complex plane algebraic curves of the same degree and with the same collection of singularities, but embedded into the plane in a topologically different way. Accordingly, such curves belong to different components of the equisingular family. This phenomenon has been intensively studied till now. In this note, we propose a different insight on this subject: Two curves $C',C''\subset\PP^2$ form an {\it anti-Zariski pair}, if $(\PP^2,C')$ and $(\PP^2,C'')$ are homeomorhic, but $C'$ and $C''$ belong to different components of the equisingular family. We exhibit examples of anti-Zariski pairs and discuss related issues.

</details>


### [21] [Symplectic duality for the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20277)

TL;DR: 本文研究了拟映射空间的上同调，该上同调将函数域 $\mathbb{F}_q(C)$ 上 $GL$ 的迷向抛物子群的几何Eisenstein级数的常数项范畴化。该上同调承载着一个对应代数的自然作用，其交换子代数是Coulomb分支上的正则函数环（此处为 $A_n$ 型曲面奇点）。曲线 $C$ 上的秩一局部系诱导了étale基本群在Coulomb分支上的作用；方案论不动点轨迹承载着一个自然向量丛。主要结果确定了在参数一般范围内，拟映射空间的上同调与该向量丛的局部上同调相同。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构造拟映射空间的上同调，研究其上的对应代数作用，利用秩一局部系诱导的étale基本群作用，分析方案论不动点轨迹上的向量丛，并在参数一般范围内建立与局部上同调的同构。

Result: 在参数一般范围内，拟映射空间的上同调与不动点轨迹上自然向量丛的局部上同调同构。

Conclusion: 建立了拟映射空间上同调与向量丛局部上同调之间的同构关系，为几何Eisenstein级数的常数项提供了上同调范畴化解释。

Abstract: We study the cohomology of a quasimap space that categorifies the constant term of the geometric Eisenstein series for the mirabolic parabolic subgroup of $GL$ over the function field $\mathbb{F}_q(C)$ of a smooth projective curve $C$. This cohomology carries a natural action of an algebra of correspondences whose commutative subalgebra is the ring of regular functions on the Coulomb branch, which here is the $A_{n}$-surface singularity. A choice of rank-one local system on $C$ induces an action of the étale fundamental group on the Coulomb branch; the scheme-theoretic fixed locus carries a natural vector bundle. Our main result identifies the cohomology of the quasimap space with the local cohomology of this vector bundle, for a generic range of parameters.

*Alexandru Dimca,Piotr Pokora*

TL;DR: 本文从数值和同调两个角度研究了线排列的Ziegler对。首先证明了当直线数量d<9时，相交格决定了本文考虑的指数数据。然后列举了六个d=10的不同Ziegler对。特别地，构造了具有相同相交格、相同Jacobian关系最小次数、相同Milnor代数Hilbert函数，但不同最小分次自由分解的高次例子。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We study Ziegler pairs of line arrangements from both numerical and homological perspectives. ### [27] [Convolution algebras associated to representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19783)
*Dragos Crisan*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究复约化群G的表示V中Borel稳定子空间M的Steinberg型簇Z，证明了在可粘合条件下，Z的等变Borel-Moore同调或K-理论（配备卷积积）可表示为两个nil-Hecke代数在其局部化中的交集，并给出了这些新代数的极点与留数描述。结果推广了Ginzburg-Kapranov-Vasserot关于仿射Hecke代数和DAHA的经典结论，以及Teleman和Gannon-Webster关于Coulomb分支的构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入"可粘合性"(gluability)条件，利用等变Borel-Moore同调/K-理论的卷积积结构，通过两个nil-Hecke代数在局部化中的交集来刻画新代数，并推广到Loop群情形。

Result: 在可粘合条件下，Z的等变Borel-Moore同调或K-理论同构于两个nil-Hecke代数拷贝在其局部化中的交集；给出了基于极点和留数的代数描述；结果同样适用于Loop群情形。

Conclusion: 该工作统一并推广了仿射Hecke代数、DAHA以及Coulomb分支等代数结构的几何构造，为表示论中相关代数的研究提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: Given a complex reductive group $G$, a representation $V$ of $G$ and a Borel-stable subspace $M \subset V$, we consider the associated Steinberg-type variety $Z$. We prove that, under a certain condition on $(V,M)$, called gluability, the equivariant Borel-Moore homology or $K$-theory of $Z$, equipped with the convolution product, is obtained as the intersection of two copies of the nil-Hecke algebra inside its localization. We also provide a description of these new algebras in terms of poles and residues. Similar results are obtained when $G$ is replaced by its loop group. This generalizes results of Ginzburg, Kapranov and Vasserot describing the affine Hecke algebra and DAHA, as well as a result of Teleman and Gannon--Webster that realizes certain Coulomb branches by gluing two copies of the universal centralizer.

### [28] [Stiefel-Whitney classes for symmetric groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19843)
*Sujeet Bhalerao,Jyotirmoy Ganguly,Steven Spallone*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了对称群S_n的表示π的Stiefel-Whitney类（SWCs）w_k(π)，证明了每个SWC是π在对合元上特征值的多项式；对于固定k，当n→∞时，不可约表示π满足w_k(π)=0的比例趋近100%；给出了首个非零SWC的简单判定准则；显式计算了前四个SWC；并给出了交错群的类似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了每个SWC是特征值的多项式；固定k时，不可约表示中w_k(π)=0的比例随n增大趋近100%；给出了首个非零SWC的显式判定准则；计算了前四个SWC；并推广到交错群。

Conclusion: 对称群表示的Stiefel-Whitney类具有多项式结构和极限消失性，且首个非零SWC可由简单准则确定，结果可推广至交错群。

Abstract: We prove several results about Stiefel-Whitney Classes (SWCs) $w_k(π)$ of representations $π$ of $S_n$. First, each SWC is polynomial in the character values of $π$ at involutions. Next, for a fixed $k$, the proportion of irreducible $π$ for which $w_k(π)=0$ approaches $100\%$ as $n \to \infty$. A similar result holds for the top SWCs. We also provide a simple criterion which determines the first nonvanishing SWC for a representation. The first four SWCs are computed explicitly. Finally, we give analogues for alternating groups.

### [29] [Characters of modules over negative rank-2 Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20386)
*Souvik Pal,Supravat Sarkar,G. Krishna Teja*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文研究了Borcherds-Kac-Moody李代数中一类新的非可积最高权模（对应新型符号主导积分锥P^±中的权μ），在秩2情形下系统分析了Verma覆盖M(μ)的模结构、极大向量及Kac-Kazhdan下界的严格性，并给出了Kac-Kazhdan方程在根锥内部有唯一解时所有模的表示和特征标公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的非可积单最高权模研究（如Naito的工作）主要局限于与P^+平移点相连的特定权μ，而近期研究发现了一类位于新型符号主导积分锥P^±中的权μ，其对应的模L(μ)具有不同于传统P^+中权模的Chevalley-Serre关系，且尚未被系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，从秩2情形入手探索这类模的结构性质。

Method: 本文采用的理论方法包括：利用Borcherds-Kac-Moody李代数在秩2情形下的结构，分析Verma覆盖M(μ)的权空间和极大向量；通过检验Kac-Kazhdan（1979）给出的线性无关极大向量个数下界的严格性或一致性等式；在Kac-Kazhdan方程于根锥内部有唯一解的条件下，推导所有模的表示和特征标公式。

Result: 获得了秩2情形下Verma覆盖M(μ)中极大向量的结构信息，明确了Kac-Kazhdan下界的严格性条件；当Kac-Kazhdan方程在根锥内部有唯一解时，给出了所有最高权模的完整表示和特征标公式。

Conclusion: 本文首次系统研究了P^±中权对应的非可积单最高权模的结构，揭示了其与经典P^+中权模的本质差异，为理解Borcherds-Kac-Moody李代数中更一般的高权模理论奠定了基础。

Abstract: Let $\mathfrak{g}=\mathfrak{g}(A)$ be the Borcherds-Kac-Moody Lie algebra (BKM LA), corresponding to a BKM Cartan matrix $A$ filled by negative integers. Let $P^+\subset \mathfrak{h}^*$ the classical dominant integral cone (wherein pairings are non-negative). The non-integrable simple highest weight modules $L(μ)$'s widely studied were broadly those by Naito ([Trans. Amer. Soc., 1995]), for $μ$'s dot-linked to $P^+$-translates of sums $- \sum_{j\in J}α_j$ of mutually orthogonal and imaginary simple roots $α_j$'s.
  Recently, we computed weights of all highest weight $\mathfrak{g}$-modules $V$'s, and characters of $L(ρ)$ for Weyl vector $ρ$ in negative type-$A$. These needed a family of ``integrable'' $L(μ)$'s for $μ$'s inside our novel signed-dominant-integral cone $P^{\pm}$ (which generalizes $P^+$). Pairings $μ(α_i^{\vee})\leq 0$ therein are multiples of $\frac{A_{ii}}{2}$ for all $i$. Nevertheless, $L(μ)$ contain ``Chevalley-Serre relations'' $f_i^{\frac{2}{A_{ii}}{μ(α_i^{\vee})}+1}L(μ)_μ=0$; which differ from relations in $L(λ)$ for all $λ\in P^+$, and are seemingly unstudied earlier (also by Naito).
  This paper initiates the study in rank-2, of the module structures and maximal vectors (or Verma embeddings) in the Verma covers $M(μ)$ of $L(μ)$'s for $μ\in P^{\pm}$. In this, our goal is to explore in weight spaces of those Verma covers, the strictness (or otherwise, an uniform equality) of lower bounds by Kac and Kazhdan ([Adv. Math., 1979]) for count of linearly independent maximal vectors. We obtain presentations and characters of all $V$'s when Kac-Kazhdan equation has unique solution in the interior of root-cone. This builds on the unique solution case in Lemma 3.1 from that paper.

</details>


### [30] [Silting t-structures in $Q$-shaped derived categories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20447)
*Anastasios Slaftsos*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文利用Saorín-Šťovíček对应，在Q-形导出范畴中通过Q的可容许划分构造了一族t-结构，证明其由silting对象诱导，并给出了明确的同调刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: t-结构（尤其是由silting/tilting对象诱导的）在三角范畴研究中具有核心地位，且与导出等价紧密相关。本文旨在Q-形导出范畴中构造具有良好性质的t-结构族。

Method: 利用Saorín-Šťovíček关于Frobenius正合范畴中余遗传余挠对与其稳定范畴中t-结构之间的对应，通过Q的可容许划分构造t-结构；在双纤维对象构成的Frobenius正合范畴中明确描述关联的余挠对，并用同调消失条件识别相应的co-aisle。

Result: 构造了一族由Q的可容许划分诱导的t-结构；证明了这些t-结构由可被Q的组合完全确定的silting对象诱导；通过恢复Q-形框架中的已知等价以及展示组合条件失效（如循环箭图）时无非平凡t-结构的情形，验证了结果。

Conclusion: 成功在Q-形导出范畴中构造了由silting对象诱导的t-结构族，揭示了与Linckelmann在稳定模范畴中观察到的现象类似的结果。

Abstract: Torsion pairs, and in particular t-structures, play a central role in the study of triangulated categories. Specifically, t-structures induced by silting (or tilting) objects often admit desirable properties with strong connections to derived equivalences. In this paper, using the correspondence of Saorín-Šťovíček between cohereditary cotorsion pairs in Frobenius exact categories and t-structures in their stable categories, we construct a family of t-structures in the $Q$-shaped derived category of Holm and Jorgensen, arising from admissible partitions of $Q$. We give an explicit description of the associated cotorsion pairs inside the Frobenius exact category of the bifibrant objects, and we identify the corresponding co-aisles by certain homological vanishing conditions. Such t-structures are proved to be induced by a silting object, that can be completely determined by the combinatorics of $Q$. Finally, we illustrate our results by recovering well-known equivalences in the $Q$-shaped setting, while also providing examples where the combinatorial conditions fail (e.g. cyclic quivers), showing that such categories may admit no non-trivial t-structures, revealing phenomena analogous to those observed by Linckelmann in stable module categories.

</details>

### [31] [Quantum circuit decomposition of the tangent-fermion Dirac operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19020)
*C. W. J. Beenakker*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格点上的狄拉克算子无法同时满足局域性、无费米子倍增和保持基本对称性。现有无倍增的非局域离散化在量子计算中会导致LCU项数和次归一化因子随格点尺寸增长，降低了量子算法的效率。

Method: 将狄拉克方程重新表述为广义特征值问题，使用局部算子铅笔（operator pencil），其中每个成员都具有精确的LCU表示，项数与格点尺寸无关，次归一化因子为O(1)量级。

Result: 切向费米子离散化避免了费米子倍增的障碍，提供了高效的块编码原语，其LCU复杂度可与椭圆算子相媲美。

Conclusion: 该方法为量子计算机上计算狄拉克谱和格林函数提供了无费米子倍增的高效实现途径。

Abstract: The Dirac operator on a lattice cannot be both local and free of fermion doubling, at least not without breaking fundamental symmetries. Non-local, symmetry-preserving discretizations that avoid doubling have a quantum circuit representation as a linear-combination-of-unitaries (LCU) in which both the number of terms and their norm (the subnormalization factor) grow with the lattice size, compromising the efficiency of a quantum algorithm. We show that the tangent-fermion discretization escapes this obstruction when the Dirac equation is written as a generalized eigenvalue problem with a local operator pencil: Each member of the pencil has an exact LCU, with term count that is independent of lattice size and with subnormalization factor of order unity, on a par with elliptic operators. This provides an efficient block-encoding primitive for Dirac spectra and Green functions without fermion doubling.

Abstract: Studies of integrable systems have profoundly deepened the fundamental understanding of quantum many-body physics. Using the tensor-network approach of the influence matrix, we develop local conditions called generalized zipper conditions that allow exact solutions of local dynamics. We also introduce a numerical bootstrap method for solving influence matrices with finite but relatively large bond dimensions. This uncovers a rich landscape of nonequilibrium behavior exhibiting initial-state dependence. As an example, we investigate the fate of persistent oscillating dynamics under local non-integrable perturbations, and present analytical results for non-thermal relaxation constrained by conservation laws. We also obtain numerically exact results for entanglement growth across a broad class of initial states. Furthermore, from an information-theoretic perspective, we identify a refined structure of multitime correlations termed the hidden Markov order: the memory encoded in the dynamics separates into finite-length and long-range distributed components, which becomes transparent in an exact split-index matrix-product-state representation of the influence matrix. Our approach enables unified investigations of nonthermalizing and thermalizing regimes of nonequilibrium dynamics within a single analytically tractable model, and can be tested experimentally in state-of-the-art quantum simulators such as Rydberg atom arrays.

We compare the resulting deformed states with those typically targeted in quantum information experiments, providing a bridge between algebraic constructions and experimentally relevant quantum resources. Fidelities with respect to the undeformed states are computed to establish how the quantum correlations are affected, both for few-qubit systems (including Dicke and non-Dicke states), and in the macroscopic limit ($N \to \infty$) through closed-form formulas derived for arbitrary Dicke states. The results reveal different behaviors between the two deformations. The $q$-deformation smoothly modifies the states and maintains a residual overlap with the original configurations, while the $h$-deformation rapidly makes the states orthogonal to their undeformed counterparts. Abstract: Photonic linear optical networks provide a versatile platform for quantum information processing and quantum state engineering. Heralding, based on conditional measurements on auxiliary modes, is a widely used technique to overcome these limitations and effectively enlarge the set of accessible states. Despite the widespread use of heralding, it is often unclear how specific ancillary resources impact the overall reachability of the target space. In this work, we investigate the local controllability of photonic states in linear optical networks by analyzing the rank of the Jacobian of the output state with respect to the underlying unitary circuit, which provides a quantitative measure of the dimension of the accessible tangent space at a given configuration. Our analysis ranges from passive linear optics to heralded linear optics, where auxiliary resources and conditional measurements are included. Within this framework, we quantify how different resources enlarge the locally accessible state space beyond that of passive linear optics and determine the resources required for the Jacobian rank to reach its maximal value, thereby achieving full local controllability. ### [39] [Nearest-neighbour gates are all you need: High-rate quantum low-density parity-check codes on a planar grid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19482)
*Boren Gu,Tamas Noszko,Vincent Steffan,Jens Niklas Eberhardt,Joschka Roffe,Jens Eisert,Stergios Koutsioumpas*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一族量子低密度奇偶校验码，首次在平面开放边界布局中结合了近邻门操作、有限尺寸优势以及恒深度稳定子测量，通过动态交换检查-数据量子比特角色实现无泄漏的容错存储，在约30个电路量子比特每逻辑量子比特下，逻辑错误率比旋转表面码低三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能量子LDPC码有望大幅降低容错量子计算的开销，但大多数构造需要长程连接或量子比特穿梭，在超导架构中难以实现。本文旨在解决这一矛盾，使量子LDPC码的优势在严格平面近邻电路中得以保留。

Method: 提出一族方向性瓦片码（directional tile codes），核心思想是通过近邻iSWAP行走动态生成检查-数据连接：iSWAP门序列既定义稳定子支撑又实现其测量，避免长程硬件图。电路实现最优常数深度稳定子测量（与码尺寸无关），并通过每轮交换检查和数据量子比特角色自然移除泄漏。

Result: 找到了如[[323,14,15]]码等有限尺寸实例，其码效率比旋转表面码高近一个数量级。在约30个电路量子比特每逻辑量子比特下，最佳方向性瓦片码布局的每逻辑每轮逻辑错误率比旋转表面码存储器低至多三个数量级（1000倍）。

Abstract: High-performance quantum low-density parity-check codes promise substantial reductions in the overhead of fault-tolerant quantum computation, but most constructions require long-range connectivity or qubit shuttling, both of which are difficult to realise in superconducting architectures. Here we introduce a family of quantum low-density parity-check codes that, for the first time, combines planar open-boundary layouts, finite-size advantages over surface codes, and syndrome extraction using only nearest-neighbour gates on a square grid of qubits. The key idea is to generate check-data connectivity dynamically: nearest-neighbour iSWAP walks both define the stabiliser supports and implement their measurement, avoiding the need for a long-range hardware graph. The resulting circuits achieve optimal constant-depth stabiliser measurement, independent of code size, and naturally remove leakage from the system by exchanging the role of check and data qubits at each syndrome extraction round. We find finite-size instances such as a [[323,14,15]] code, whose code-efficiency ratio is nearly an order of magnitude larger than that of rotated surface-code patches. At around 30 circuit qubits per logical qubit, the best directional tile-code layouts reduce the per-logical per-round logical error rate by up to a factor of 1000 relative to rotated surface-code memories. These results show that the advantages of quantum low-density parity-check codes can survive compilation into strictly planar nearest-neighbour circuits, bringing low-overhead fault-tolerant memories closer to near-term hardware.

### [40] [Random Local Stabilizer Codes in Three Dimensions without String or Self-Similar Fractal Logical Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19873)
*Han Yan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了qutrit随机立方码——一类具有空间变化稳定子的局域qutrit CSS稳定子哈密顿量，证明了其无弦性质，并通过数值观察发现其相比于平移不变分形码具有不同的性质：最小基态简并指数为k=2（奇L）或k=4（偶L），非收缩平面逻辑算子跨越整个逻辑空间，且电荷推诊断表明不存在自相似分形逻辑算子。结果表明约束随机性可以从根本上改变稳定子码的性质并改善其自校正特性。

Method: 提出qutrit随机立方码（qutrit random cubic codes），这是一类局域qutrit CSS稳定子哈密顿量族，具有与Haah Code 1相似的立方体检查结构，但稳定子是空间变化的（spatially varying stabilizers），打破了平移不变性。

Result: 1) 证明了该模型保留无弦性质；2) 数值观察到基态简并指数：奇L时k=2，偶L时k=4；3) 非收缩平面逻辑算子跨越整个逻辑空间；4) 电荷推诊断表明自相似分形逻辑算子消失；5) 约束随机性可改变稳定子码的性质并改善自校正特性。

Conclusion: 约束随机性可以从根本上改变稳定子码的性质，改善其自校正特性，并指向超越典型拓扑序和分形序的更广泛量子纠错码和量子相家族。

Abstract: Quantum error-correcting codes (QECs) are essential components quantum computation and have deep connections to quantum phases of matter. A key obstruction to passive self-correcting QECs is the presence of string logical operators, which can generate logical errors through constant-energy-barrier processes. Haah's Codes (fracton codes) showed that three-dimensional stabilizer codes can forbid such string logical operators, but their translation-invariant structure supports self-similar fractal logical operators with a logarithmic energy barrier. We introduce the qutrit random cubic codes, a family of local qutrit Calderbank-Shor-Steane stabilizer Hamiltonians with similar cube-check structure as Haah's Code 1 but built from spatially varying stabilizers. We prove that these models retain the no-string property and numerically observe that they have properties distinct from translation-invariant fracton codes: the smallest ground-state degeneracy exponent is $k=2$ for odd $L$ and $k=4$ for even $L$; noncontractible plane-logical operators span the entire logical space; and charge-push diagnostics show that the self-similar fractal operators are absent. These results demonstrate that constrained randomness can fundamentally change the nature of stabilizer codes and improve their self-correction properties. They further point to broader families of quantum error-correcting codes and quantum phases beyond canonical topological and fracton orders.

### [41] [Optimal Ansatz-free Hamiltonian Learning In Situ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19486)
*Taiqi Zhou,Weiyuan Gong*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需控制、无需辅助比特的哈密顿量学习算法，仅使用泡利积态制备与测量，在总演化时间 Θ(Λ/ε² log(Λ/ε)) 内实现无假设哈密顿量学习，并证明该时间代价在无控制协议中是最优的。该方法引入随机采样框架，结合带限核时域采样与位移筛进行结构学习，特征探测时间分辨率仅依赖于 Λ 而非 ε，特别适合高精度传感与校准场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有最优哈密顿量学习协议虽达到海森堡极限缩放，但依赖于深度交错探测与控制电路以及极短时间分辨率，难以在近期和中期的原位量子实验中实现。因此需要一种实验上友好、无需控制、无需辅助比特且计算高效的哈密顿量学习算法。

Method: 提出随机采样框架，结合带限核（band-limited kernel）的时域采样方法与位移筛（displacement sieve）进行哈密顿量结构学习；仅使用泡利积态制备与测量，无需控制脉冲或辅助量子比特。

Result: 总演化时间代价为 Θ(Λ/ε² log(Λ/ε))，并证明该下界 Ω(Λ/ε² log(Λ/ε)) 对任何无控制协议都是最优的。特征探测时间分辨率仅取决于 Λ 而非 ε，在高精度下具有显著优势。存在SPAM噪声时，若哈密顿量局部可校准，算法仍保持相同渐近总演化时间。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了实验友好型哈密顿量学习的基本代价，为近期量子平台的严格原位表征提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Characterizing the features of a Hamiltonian that governs a quantum system serves as a fundamental subroutine of quantum device calibration, signal sensing, and error correction. Recent works proposed protocols have achieved the optimal Heisenberg-limited scaling learning ansatz-free Hamiltonians from their real-time evolutions without fully specifying interaction structures. However, these protocols rely on both deep circuits with interleaving probes and control, and extremely short time resolution, making them difficult to implement on near- and intermediate-term in situ quantum experiments. In this work, we propose a computationally efficient, control-free, and ancilla-free algorithm that uses only Pauli product state preparation and measurement, and learns an ansatz-free Hamiltonian $H$ with $||H||\leqΛ$ in total evolution time of $Θ(\fracΛ{ε^2}\log(\fracΛε))$. The evolution time cost of our algorithm is optimal for any control-free protocols as we further prove a lower bound of $Ω(\fracΛ{ε^2}\log(\fracΛε))$. Technically, our method introduces a randomized-sampling framework that combines band-limited kernel-based time sampling with a displacement sieve for Hamiltonian structure learning. The characteristic probe time resolution depends only on $Λ$ instead of $\varepsilon$, which makes our protocol especially appealing in the high-precision regime for sensing and calibration applications. We also show that the algorithm maintains the same asymptotic total evolution time in the presence of state-preparation-and-measurement (SPAM) noise when the Hamiltonian is local after calibration. Our results demonstrate the fundamental cost of experimentally friendly Hamiltonian learning and provide a practical route to rigorous in situ characterization of near-term quantum platforms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We reconstruct unitary quantum dynamics from a minimal axiomatic foundation built on Hilbert-space observables and isospectral evolution. The only dynamical assumption is that physical time evolution is a continuous one-parameter flow of Hermitian observables that preserves their spectra, i.e. the possible outcomes of measurement. We show that this assumption is already sufficient to force the Lax form of quantum dynamics. The Heisenberg equation, the time-dependent and time-independent Schrödinger equations, conservation laws, and good quantum numbers then follow as theorems rather than postulates. In this formulation, Lax pair theory supplies the missing dynamical bridge between the measurement structure of a Hilbert space and standard quantum evolution: the Hamiltonian is not assumed, but emerges as the generator required for an isospectral observable flow.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: For quantum algorithms to achieve their full potential, we need methodologies to optimize them, such as reaching a given output accuracy with minimal resource costs. Here, we develop such a methodology for a class of Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) algorithms. We leverage simulations of a Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) to propose a phenomenological model of such algorithms that captures the complex relationship between algorithmic accuracy, algorithmic resource costs, and the noise that exists in realistic quantum hardware. For this, we take the algorithmic resource cost to be the total number of quantum gate-operations in the algorithm; minimizing this cost typically makes the algorithm faster and more energy-efficient. We consider the subtle trade-off between quantum circuit size (small circuits are too imprecise, but large ones are too noisy), and the number of iterations of that quantum circuit for the full algorithm to sufficiently converge. Using a noise-metric-resource methodology, we identify the sweet spot (of circuit size versus iterations) that minimizes the algorithmic resource costs for a desired algorithm accuracy. It also gives the circuit size that maximizes algorithm accuracy for a fixed resource cost. Our methodology provides a practical guideline for near-term deployment of variational algorithms on realistic noisy hardware, including hardware that uses error mitigation.

Here, we examine this relationship through the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), a specific class of variational algorithms, applied to the MaxCut problem. We show that suboptimal variational parameter training can significantly modify the observed entanglement profile, obscuring its scaling behavior. By employing a high-performance optimizer, we find empirical evidence that QAOA exhibits entanglement scaling consistent with that of fermionic Gaussian states (up to a scaling factor) across a broad range of MaxCut instances. We further compare these results with adiabatic quantum computation, observing annealing-schedule-dependent entanglement profiles whose scaling behavior differs markedly from that of QAOA. Together, these findings provide new insight into how entanglement manifests in and distinguishes these two algorithmic paradigms, highlighting its connection to both computational performance and application structure.

### [45] [Vine Codes: Low-Overhead Quantum LDPC Codes on a Planar Square Grid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20263)
*Georgia M. Nixon,Campbell K. McLauchlan,Charles C. L. van Rest*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出Vine Codes，一种可在超导平面方格上通过最近邻两量子比特门实现的qLDPC码，相比表面码可减少约18-28%的量子比特开销，并在10^{-3}噪声率下表现更优。同时引入Flip-Vine Codes支持单量子比特横向Clifford门，并探索了超越传统X/Z边界的广义开放边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面码需要大量量子比特开销，而现有qLDPC码虽能降低开销但需要长程连接，难以在超导平台上实现。本文旨在设计既保持低开销优势又能在平面方格上通过最近邻门实现的qLDPC码。

Method: 将"Directional Codes"从环面约束推广到开放边界条件，引入路由量子比特在平面方格上构建Vine Codes；通过数值搜索寻找候选码；引入Flip-Vine Codes实现横向Clifford门；构造广义开放边界。

Result: 找到[[121,4,6]]、[[221,6,7]]、[[234,9,6]]等候选码；电路距离7时数据和测量量子比特减少约28%；包含路由比特后总量子比特仍比表面码少约18%（电路距离10）；在10^{-3}噪声率下性能优于表面码。

Conclusion: Vine Codes在超导平台上实现了qLDPC码的低开销优势，为容错量子计算提供了更高效的编码方案，且支持容错逻辑门和魔法态培育，具有实际应用前景。

Abstract: The surface code is a promising route towards large-scale quantum computing, requiring only nearest-neighbour gates amenable to superconducting hardware. However, surface codes incur large qubit overheads. Novel quantum low-density parity check (qLDPC) codes promise to reduce overheads but require long-range connections that are difficult to achieve on superconducting platforms. Here, we introduce "Vine Codes" - qLDPC codes that are implementable on a planar square grid through nearest-neighbour, two-qubit gates native to superconducting platforms (iSWAP and CZ). Our approach generalises "Directional Codes" recently introduced by Gehér et. al. (2025) which are constrained to a torus. In contrast, vine codes have open boundary conditions constructed with the aid of routing qubits. We perform extensive numeric searches and find promising candidate vine codes, e.g. [[121,4,6]], [[221,6,7]], and [[234,9,6]] codes. We verify the circuit distances and show that data and measure qubits required can be reduced by up to ~28% relative to the surface code at a circuit distance of 7. Even including routing qubits, vine codes require fewer total qubits than the surface code (e.g. ~18% reduction at circuit distance 10) and benefits are expected to increase at higher distances. We perform circuit-level noise simulations to demonstrate that under a realistic noise model and at a near-term noise rate of $10^{-3}$, vine codes can perform better than the surface code while using fewer qubits. We give an exhaustive list of all unique vine codes up to stabiliser-weight 9. We additionally introduce "Flip-Vine Codes" which possess single-qubit transversal Clifford gates useful for fault-tolerant logic and magic state cultivation. We furthermore construct examples of generalised open boundaries for vine codes that go beyond the familiar X/Z boundaries of the surface and tile codes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 物理正则能量条件下开放系统的存活概率呈亚线性衰变，而任意耗散GKLS半群呈线性短时间衰变，两者不可兼容。

We show that this description cannot be exact under physically regular energy conditions. We prove that the open-system survival probability under physically regular energy conditions has sublinear decay, whereas any dissipative GKLS semigroup has a linear short-time decay. Hence exact Markovian dissipation requires singular energy resources: an unbounded-below total Hamiltonian or infinite initial energy, and a divergent interaction-energy moment. Therefore, a dissipative time-independent GKLS equation should be regarded as an effective description rather than the exact reduced dynamics of a Hamiltonian dilation satisfying physically regular energy conditions.

Abstract: Unlike in closed quantum systems where individual energy eigenstates are understood as physical excitations, open quantum systems have distinct right and left eigenstates of the Liouvillian that decay with time and are difficult to interpret. Here we introduce a physically motivated quasiprobability measure combining the two types of eigenstates that interprets a Liouville eigenmode as a set of coherences. This coherence measure is intimately connected to the return probability and allows one to visualize the modes as quasiprobability distributions in a "doubled" phase space. Using this measure we show that, remarkably, an oscillator retains its quantized "orbits" in phase space for a large class of linear and nonlinear damping, thus providing a formulation of semiclassical quantization for open systems. The orbits have measurable dynamical signatures and are broadened in the presence of a thermal bath, similar to energy levels.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多时间量子过程的区分是诊断、基准测试和学习时间相关量子动力学的基础任务。标准策略范数距离虽是最优基准，但需要大量相干记忆和时变控制，实际实现困难。本文旨在引入一种更实用、可扩展且具有相干记忆约束的区分框架。

Method: 提出自主区分机器（MADs）：在每个时间步应用相同量子仪器，保留完整经典结果记录，并携带d_A维相干记忆。通过优化这些策略定义记忆参数化的可区分性度量d^{(N)}_{MAD}。证明了该层次结构在相干记忆上单调且有限时间内完备，即可将任意N步探测策略编译为带内部计数器和足够大相干记忆的单个MAD。对于重复系统-环境相互作用产生的循环过程，推导了单步描述以分离新区分信息的生成与旧信息的传播衰减。

Result: 在重复相互作用模型中的数值结果表明，增加相干记忆系统地提高了MAD的成功概率，缩小了与策略范数距离的差距，同时计算复杂度显著更低。层次结构最终能饱和策略范数距离基准。

Conclusion: MAD可区分性为量化在有限相干记忆下能从真正多时间量子过程中学到什么提供了可操作且可扩展的框架。

Abstract: Distinguishing multi-time quantum processes is a fundamental task underlying the diagnosis, benchmarking, and learning of temporally correlated quantum dynamics. The standard benchmark for distinguishing two processes is the strategy-norm distance, which optimizes over arbitrary adaptive probing strategies but can require large coherent memory and time-dependent control. We introduce machines for autonomous distinction~($\mathsf{MAD}$s): probing strategies that apply the same quantum instrument at each time step, retain the full classical outcome record, and carry a coherent memory of dimension $d_A$. Optimizing over these strategies defines a memory-parametrized distinguishability measure, $d^{(N)}_{\mathsf{MAD}}(\mathbf{P}^N,\mathbf{Q}^N;d_A)$. We show that the resulting hierarchy is monotone in coherent memory and complete at finite times. Specifically, any admissible $N$-step probing strategy can be compiled into a single $\mathsf{MAD}$ with an internal counter and sufficiently large coherent memory, so the hierarchy saturates the strategy-norm benchmark. For recurrent processes generated by repeated system--environment interactions, we derive a single-step description that separates the generation of new distinguishing information from the propagation and decay of information generated at earlier times. Numerical results in a repeated-interaction model show that increasing coherent memory systematically improves the $\mathsf{MAD}$ success probability and closes the gap to the strategy-norm distance while remaining substantially more tractable to evaluate. $\mathsf{MAD}$ distinguishability therefore provides an operational and scalable framework for quantifying what can be learned about genuinely multi-time quantum processes with bounded coherent memory.

</details>


### [49] [Optimal Shadow Estimation with Minimal Measurement Settings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20003)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前已知3-设计可实现最坏情况最优阴影估计，但所需的最小测量基数量一直未明确。本文旨在填补这一理论空白，同时探索平均情况下的性能下界，揭示最坏情况与平均情况之间的复杂性分离。

Method: 利用群论和设计理论，证明Θ(d²)个测量基对最坏情况最优性既是必要的也是充分的，并构造显式基族。对于平均情况，证明任意态2-设计已足够，分析平均阴影范数的上界，并证明Haar随机态的强集中性。

Conclusion: 建立了阴影估计中基复杂度的根本性分离：最坏情况与平均情况之间相差一个维度因子，对量子信息理论和近期实验设计有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Shadow estimation is a powerful framework for predicting quantum properties from randomized measurements. While $3$-design protocols achieve optimal worst-case performance, the minimal number of measurement bases required for such optimality has remained open. Here we prove that $Θ(d^2)$ measurement bases are both necessary and sufficient for worst-case optimal shadow estimation and construct an explicit basis family. In stark contrast, any state $2$-design already suffices for average-case optimality: the mean squared shadow norm of normalized observables is bounded by a universal constant, and we prove strong concentration for Haar-random states, yielding constant sample complexity for generic pure-state fidelity estimation. Easily implementable $2$-designs -- from mutually unbiased bases, cyclic measurements, or shallow $\mathcal{O}(\log n)$-depth circuits -- enable optimal average-case protocols with remarkably simple measurement strategies. Our results establish a fundamental complexity separation: worst-case estimation requires $Θ(d^2)$ bases, whereas average-case performance requires only $Θ(d)$ bases, with broad implications for quantum information theory and near-term experiments.

*Santiago Cifuentes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该问题属于QCMA，且若属于BQP则NP ⊆ BQP。即使在ρ为纯态且ε为常数的情况下也成立。

We consider that the state $ρ$ is described as the result of tracing out some of the qubits of a pure state prepared by a circuit $C$, and we assume the promise that either there is a Pauli matrix satisfying the stated condition or, instead, that for all non-identity Pauli matrices $P$ it is the case that $|Tr(Pρ)|\leq \varepsilon/2$. The problem is in $QCMA$, and we prove that if it belongs to $BQP$ then $NP \subseteq BQP$. The result is obtained through a reduction from the minimum-weight code problem, and it holds even when $ρ$ is assumed to be a pure state (i.e. when no qubits are discarded) and $\varepsilon$ is constant. This resolves an open question regarding the existence of efficient tomographic procedures to find the largest coefficients of a quantum state in the Pauli basis: namely, they do not exist under the standard hypothesis $NP \nsubseteq BQP$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在均匀独立选择条件下，Alice只能获知复合操作U_eff=U2U1，而各因子U1和U2代数上保持隐藏；有效复合操作充当奇偶约束，每个被动用户可结合自身私密选择推断对方操作，而主动站仅知全局组合；方案主要受限于Bell态测量的成功概率。

Abstract: We propose and analyze a Bell-state extension of the Loop-Back quantum key distribution architecture for secret-key establishment between two passive users that do not require quantum transmitters or quantum detectors. In the proposed setting, a single active station, Alice, provides the entangled-state infrastructure, retains one qubit of an initially prepared Bell pair, and sends the traveling subsystem through two passive users, denoted by $B_1$ and $B_2$. Each passive user applies a local Pauli operation to the same traveling subsystem, so that the operation observed by Alice is only the effective composition $U_{\mathrm{eff}}=U_2U_1$. After the subsystem returns, Alice performs a Bell-state measurement and, using her private knowledge of the initial Bell state, deterministically identifies the effective Pauli operation. However, the individual factors $U_1$ and $U_2$ remain algebraically hidden from Alice whenever the local choices are uniformly and independently selected. The public effective operation acts as a parity-like constraint: each passive user can infer the operation applied by the other from its own private choice, while the active station learns only the global composition. This construction transfers the essential distributed-transformation mechanism of passive-user Loop-Back QKD to the entangled-state regime. Unlike single-qubit passive-user schemes, whose useful events are intrinsically post-selected, the Bell-state version is limited primarily by the success probability of the Bell-state measurement. We discuss the algebraic structure of the protocol, its interpretation as an infrastructure-assisted mediated key-establishment mechanism, and the physical assumptions required to protect passive Pauli modulators against active injection or Trojan-horse-type attacks.

The central examples are power-of-$p$ graphs, where even and odd values of $p$ exhibit qualitatively distinct behaviour: even-$p$ graphs inherit the rich phase structure of the power-of-two model, while odd-$p$ graphs are governed by geometric frustration. Fibonacci graphs provide a contrasting case, lacking the discrete self-similarity of the power-of-$p$ family but exhibiting a direct geometric mapping between the short- and long-range limits. Across our models, we find that phase structure and criticality are governed by the same effective-geometry principle, unifying our framework for experimentally motivated long-range quantum systems.

Abstract: A defining feature of chirality is the distinction between a system and its mirror image. Despite extensive experimental observations of chiral phases and theoretical advances, a quantum-information theoretic characterization of chirality based solely on the entanglement structure of many-body quantum states remains elusive. Here, we introduce the notion of many-body chirality by formulating it as an obstruction to transforming a quantum state into its complex conjugate through finite-depth local operations. We rigorously establish many-body chirality for stabilizer realizations of $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ anyon theories, proving that complex conjugation can be implemented by local quantum channels if and only if the underlying anyon data are mirror invariant. This reveals forms of chirality that evade conventional diagnostics, including examples with vanishing modular commutator, vanishing chiral central charge, and commuting-projector realizations. We further show that this obstruction is intrinsically four-partite, while invisible to tripartite entanglement structure. Finally, we prove that $\mathbb{Z}_d^{(k)}$ states with $d>2$ possess intrinsic many-body imaginarity: their complex phase structure cannot be removed by finite-depth local unitaries. Remarkably, this includes states that are not many-body chiral.

*Sara Tarquini,Matteo Vandelli,Francesco Ferrari,Daniele Dragoni,Francesco Tudisco*

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种混合量子-经典近似框架，利用中性原子量子计算机作为独立集采样器来解决灾难响应中的应急操作中心选址问题（最小支配集问题），在Pasqal的Fresnel量子处理器上实现了多达100个节点的实例求解，结果表明即使在硬件噪声下，量子生成的样本也能实现接近最优的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在灾难响应中，需要选择最少数量的应急操作中心（枢纽），确保所有受灾地点在目标响应时间内得到覆盖。这一问题可形式化为图上的最小支配集问题，传统方法在规模增大时面临计算挑战，而量子计算有望提供新的求解途径。

Method: 提出混合量子-经典近似框架：利用中性原子量子计算机作为独立集采样器，从小最大独立集和大独立集的补集中构建候选支配集，随后通过轻量级经典过程进行精炼优化。

Result: 在合成实例和真实案例研究上进行基准测试，并在Pasqal的Fresnel量子处理器上实现，求解了多达100个节点的实例。结果表明，尽管存在硬件噪声，量子生成的样本仍能实现接近最优的解决方案。

Conclusion: 证明了以模拟模式运行的中性原子设备已经可以用于解决现实世界应用中的图优化问题。

Abstract: We study the problem of emergency operation center placement in disaster response, where a minimal number of hubs must be selected to ensure timely coverage of all affected locations. This task can be formulated as a minimum dominating set problem on a graph encoding reachability within a target response time. We propose a hybrid quantum-classical approximation framework that leverages neutral-atom quantum computers as independent set samplers. Candidate dominating sets are constructed from both small maximal independent sets and complements of large independent sets, and are subsequently refined via a lightweight classical procedure. We benchmark the approach on synthetic instances and realistic case studies, and implement it on the Fresnel quantum processor by Pasqal, solving instances of up to 100 nodes. Our results show that quantum-generated samples, despite hardware noise, enable near-optimal solutions of the placement problem. Overall, our results demonstrate that neutral-atom devices operating in analog mode can already be used to tackle graph optimization problems for real-world applications.

</details>


### [58] [Topological Codes Based on Space Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20548)
*Chong-Yuan Xu,Ze-Chuan Liu,Yong Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的拓扑码大多假设平移不变性，这限制了拓扑码的构造可能性。作者希望引入点群操作来扩展拓扑码的设计空间，探索更具一般性的拓扑码构造。

Method: 作者构造了一类CSS码——空间群码，其校验算子基于空间群（平移与点群操作的组合）上的群代数模板构建。利用环模及其不变量理论分析拓扑性质。

Result: 空间群码虽然看似实现更复杂，但实际上可以比纯平移码表现出更好的局域性，从而扩展了拓扑码的设计空间。

Abstract: Topological codes form one of the most important classes of stabilizer codes. Most existing algebraic constructions and analyses of topological codes assume translation invariance. Here we show that topological codes can arise in more general settings by incorporating point group operations. The central construction is a class of Calderbank-Shor-Steane (CSS) codes called space-group codes, whose check operators are built from group-algebra templates over space groups that combine translations with point-group operations. We develop methods for analyzing topological properties of space-group codes using ring-modules and their invariant theory. At first glance, space-group codes might appear to complicate practical implementation; however, we find that they can exhibit greater locality than previous codes based purely on translations. Our framework thus extends the landscape of topological codes and opens up a broader design space for the co-design of topological codes with quantum computing platforms.

### [59] [Stalls and Spequlation: Pipelined Execution for Fault Tolerant Quantum Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19593)
*Aditi Awasthi,Gokul Subramanian Ravi,Jonathan Mark Baker*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于容错量子计算的流水线执行框架，将逻辑操作分解为控制、执行和解码三个阶段，并通过推测策略允许后继操作在前序操作完成解码前开始执行。实验表明，推测性流水线相比无推测基线可减少20-40%的流水线步骤，并且最激进的策略在大多数情况下表现最优，尽管需要部分回滚，但回滚代价远小于并行性带来的收益。此外，推测策略还能有效平衡异构子系统间的负载，将空闲时间转化为有效计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的容错量子计算调度模型将逻辑操作视为原子操作，忽略了经典控制逻辑、量子硬件和经典错误解码器这三个子系统实际是顺序执行且存在大量空闲时间的问题，导致资源利用率低下。

Method: 提出流水线执行框架，将每个逻辑操作分解为控制（Control）、执行（Execute）和解码（Decode）三个阶段，并设计了多种推测策略（speculation strategies），允许后继操作在前序操作完成解码前就开始处理。

Result: 在多个常见基准测试上，推测性流水线相比无推测基线减少20-40%的流水线步骤；最激进的策略持续优于保守策略，尽管需要部分回滚，但回滚惩罚相对于获得的并行度增益很小；推测策略还能通过跨异构子系统均衡工作负载，将空闲时间转化为有效计算。

Conclusion: 流水线执行框架结合推测策略能有效提升容错量子计算系统的执行效率，减少空闲时间，并实现更好的负载均衡。

Abstract: Fault-tolerant quantum computation requires the coordinated action of three distinct systems: classical control logic, quantum hardware, and classical error decoders. Current scheduling models treat logical operations as atomic, hiding the fact that these subsystems operate sequentially and spend significant time idle. We present a pipelined execution framework that decomposes each logical operation into its component stages i.e. Control, Execute, and Decode. Building on this, we discuss some speculation strategies that allow successor operations to begin processing before their predecessors have completed decoding. We evaluate our framework on several common benchmarks and show that pipelining with speculation reduces total pipeline steps by 20-40% compared to a no-speculation baseline. The most aggressive strategy consistently outperforms conservative alternatives, even though partial rollback is needed at times, because the per-rollback penalty is small relative to the parallelism gained. We further show that speculation facilitates load balancing by distributing work more evenly across the heterogeneous subsystems of a fault-tolerant quantum computer, converting idle time into useful computation while also saving on execution time.

Method: 通过数值优化量子Fisher信息，在损耗和相位噪声的联合参数空间中搜索最优量子态，并与高斯态的性能进行比较。

These fall into three classes: Fock-like, cubic-phase-like, and states with discrete rotational symmetry. Abstract: We study a family of sparse positive maps on qutrits for which positivity, decomposability, and PPT entanglement can all be analysed explicitly. The block structure of the associated Choi matrices reduces positivity to a Hermitian biquadratic form and leads to exact positivity boundaries for three representative parametric families. The first consists of witness-adapted deformations naturally tied to the non-decomposability analysis. The second consists of analytically tractable families whose full PPT-entangled branch is detected by fixed positive maps, yielding exact thresholds between separability and bound entanglement. Abstract: Topological waveguide arrays support robust mode propagation in the presence of fabrication imperfections, providing a significant advantage for on-chip quantum information processing. However, this robustness does not fully extend to nonlinear biphoton generation. Structural disorder can enhance the excitation of non-topological biphoton modes during nonlinear interactions, which degrades the quantum properties of the generated state. To overcome this limitation, we propose an adiabatic passage that connects an isolated site to a topological defect array. By initiating the nonlinear process in a strongly isolated regime, nonlinear coupling to unwanted modes is effectively suppressed, thereby preserving the Schmidt number of the generated state. The subsequent adiabatic connection facilitates the high fidelity transfer of the generated biphoton into the topological biphoton mode. ### [65] [QMCtwin: Master-Equation Simulation of Syndrome Statistics Beyond Pauli Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19848)
*Tong Shen,Huo Chen,Benchen Huang,Tyler Takeshita,Arian Vezvaee,Izhar Medalsy,Daniel A. Lidar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出QMCtwin，一个无符号问题量子蒙特卡洛框架，用于主方程仿真量子纠错电路。通过距离-7旋转表面码(97个物理量子比特)的完整综合征提取实验，发现包含超导设备真实噪声机制(弛豫、退相、门校准误差、残余ZZ串扰、驱动量子比特失谐)的主方程动力学与其Pauli-twirled Clifford仿真对应物之间存在显著偏差，揭示了传统Pauli噪声模型隐藏的综合征提取偏差和相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错向大规模实验推进过程中，解码器性能日益依赖于硬件噪声如何忠实映射到综合征统计量。标准稳定子工作流通过将设备动力学替换为随机Pauli或探测器误差模型实现可扩展性，但这种压缩可能丢弃相干相位信息、非幺正漂移、始终耦合的连续时间效应以及哈密顿量与耗散同时演化产生的相关性。

Method: 提出QMCtwin框架，利用无符号问题量子蒙特卡洛方法进行主方程仿真；构建包含超导设备噪声机制的开放系统模型(弛豫、纯退相、相干门校准误差、残余ZZ串扰、驱动量子比特失谐)；直接估计综合征可观测量并与Pauli-twirled Clifford仿真进行对比；引入信息论诊断量化两种模型间的信息差异。

Result: QMCtwin预测了在随机Pauli描述中缺失或强烈抑制的综合征提取偏差以及综合征与逻辑弦奇偶代理之间的相关性；信息论诊断进一步量化了真实主方程仿真与Pauli-twirled模型之间关于综合征与弦奇偶代理信息的差异。

Conclusion: 基于QMC的主方程数字孪生能够揭示传统Pauli/Clifford噪声模型隐藏的噪声特征，为构建更准确的面向解码器的综合征模型提供了实用路径。

Abstract: As quantum error correction moves toward large-scale experimental implementations, decoder performance increasingly depends on how faithfully hardware noise is translated into syndrome statistics. Standard stabilizer workflows achieve scalability by replacing device dynamics with stochastic Pauli or detector-error models, but this compression can discard coherent phase information, nonunital drift, continuous-time effects of always-on couplings, and correlations generated by simultaneous Hamiltonian and dissipative evolution. Here we present QMCtwin, a sign-problem-suppressed quantum Monte Carlo framework for master-equation simulation of QEC circuits, and apply it to a full syndrome-extraction round of a distance-$7$ rotated surface code with $97$ physical qubits. The open-system model includes realistic superconducting-device noise mechanisms such as relaxation, pure dephasing, coherent gate miscalibration, residual $ZZ$ crosstalk, and drive-qubit detuning. By directly estimating syndrome observables from the QMC-generated stochastic density matrix estimator, we compare the master-equation dynamics with their Pauli-twirled Clifford simulation counterparts. QMCtwin predicts syndrome-extraction biases and correlations between syndromes and proxies of logical-string-parity that are absent or strongly suppressed in the stochastic Pauli description. We introduce information-theoretic diagnostics that further quantify how information concerning syndromes versus string-parity proxies differs between the realistic master-equation simulation and the corresponding Pauli-twirled model. These results show that QMC-based master-equation digital twins can expose noise features hidden by conventional Pauli/Clifford noise models and provide a practical path toward more accurate decoder-facing syndrome models.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate ancilla-assisted work extraction in quantum batteries from the perspective of bound energy and purity. We show that the bound energy of the reduced system provides a tight upper bound to the daemonic gain and that this bound is saturated for globally pure system--ancilla states. Motivated by this relation, we introduce a purity-based gain that qualitatively predicts the daemonic gain without requiring explicit optimization over measurements. We further introduce a protocol to analyze the role of dissipation and intrinsic interactions on daemonic gain. Under a collective environment, dissipation can dynamically generate and stabilize finite daemonic gain through environment-induced correlations. In interacting systems, level crossings and spectral restructuring strongly modify the attainable gain through their influence on the accessible bound energy. Our results demonstrate that daemonic gain is governed not only by correlations, but also by the spectral structure of the underlying Hamiltonian and information loss captured by bound energy and purity.

### [67] [QMaxCal: Path-Space Regularization for Open Quantum Control via Girsanov's Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19947)
*Merijn Moody,Zier Mensch,Miranda C. N. Cheng,Peter G. Bolhuis,Max Welling*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出两种基于Girsanov定理的正则化方法（Wiener KL散度和漂移方差正则化），用于优化开放量子系统在连续监测下的控制策略，通过惩罚退相干通道的观测后果而非控制幅度本身，在单/多量子比特基准测试和IBM Kingston处理器校准链上实现了高达50%的保真度提升和27个百分点的噪声鲁棒性增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在存在退相干的情况下实现可靠的量子控制，需要能够对抗环境噪声影响的策略。现有方法主要惩罚控制幅度或平滑度，而非直接针对退相干效应本身。

Method: 利用Girsanov定理，基于连续监测下开放量子系统经典测量记录的漂移差异，构建KL散度的封闭形式可微估计器。实例化两种物理驱动的正则化项：Wiener KL散度（KL_W）和漂移方差正则化（R_DV），两者均直接惩罚控制对退相干通道的可观测后果。

Result: 在单/多量子比特基准测试和IBM Kingston处理器校准链上，正则化方法在最终态保真度、噪声模型失配鲁棒性（训练噪声下+17pp，2.5倍失配下+27pp）和禁止态占据等指标上均优于未正则化的梯度方法和强化学习基线。不保真度降低高达50%，IBM Kingston链上增益约16%。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于轨迹分布KL散度的正则化方法能有效抑制退相干效应，比传统控制幅度惩罚方法更优，且对不同噪声模型具有良好普适性。

Abstract: Reliable quantum control in the presence of decoherence requires policies that combat the effect of environmental noise on the controlled dynamics. Open quantum systems under continuous monitoring generate classical measurement records whose drift depends on the noise experienced by the system; the records of two evolutions sharing the same decoherence channels differ only in this drift, so Girsanov's theorem yields a closed-form, differentiable estimator of the KL divergence between their trajectory distributions. We instantiate this estimator with two physically motivated reference measures, yielding two regularizers that both drive the system toward states where the effects of decoherence are minimal: the Wiener KL (KL_W), which is empirically more effective under certain conditions on the noise model, and the drift-variance regularizer (R_DV), which works for all noise models. Both are qualitatively distinct from existing penalties on control fluence or smoothness: they penalize the observable consequences of control on the decoherence channels rather than the control amplitude itself. The regularizers outperform unregularized gradient-based and reinforcement-learning baselines across a range of open quantum systems -- including single- and multi-qubit benchmarks and a multi-qubit chain calibrated to a published snapshot of the IBM Kingston processor -- along several axes of evaluation: final-state fidelity, robustness to mismatch in the assumed noise model (gains grow from +17 pp at training noise to +27 pp under 2.5x noise mismatch), and occupation of forbidden states. The regularizers reduce infidelity by up to 50%, with ~16% gains on the calibrated IBM Kingston chain.

We demonstrate that the mutual influence of long-range pairing exponent, chemical potential, and inter-leg coupling strength gives rise to a rich topological phase diagram characterized by multiple Majorana zero modes and massive Dirac modes. In particular, we show that the inter-leg coupling renormalizes the effective energy scales, leading to a systematic shift of the topological phase boundaries and enabling controlled tuning of the Majorana modes. Furthermore, we identify a transition from a two Majorana zero mode phase to a phase encapsulating four Majorana zero modes, as the long-range pairing exponent is varied. This transition is accompanied by a crossover regime in which Majorana zero modes coexist with massive Dirac modes, reflecting hybridization between edge and bulk excitations. This ladder thus provides a minimal and attractive platform for realizing the impact of a long-range pairing on topological phases. Our results highlight the potential of long-range hybrid systems for engineering tunable topological states relevant for quantum information applications.

By incorporating simulated annealing to escape gradient-vanishing plateaus, our framework achieves a design success rate of nearly 60 % for photon blockade with g2(0) smaller than 0.1 and theoretically bounded brightness across a broad parameter space, without any analytical guidance. This framework provides a general recipe for multi-objective design of open quantum systems.

The most general framework for this optimization relies on agnostic, off-the-shelf machine-learning techniques. Here we take the opposite approach: by focusing on a physical description of the specific optical process, we develop a deterministic sequential algorithm that provably reaches the global maximum of the visibility in a pixel basis and scales linearly with the number of pixels, thereby offering an efficient and theoretically grounded alternative to black-box optimization.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的多副本量子态非线性性质测量协议（如swap测试）需要对完整希尔伯特空间进行相干操作，对于大系统实验上不可行。因此需要一种能够根据硬件能力灵活调整相干资源消耗的测量方案。

Method: 在集体测量前引入随机投影，将n-qubit量子态压缩到q-qubit子空间，然后仅在降维后的希尔伯特空间上执行集体测量。通过分析Haar平均下的投影矩与原始态多变量迹之间的关系，推导了采样开销与投影维度之间的定量关系。

Result: 估计tr(ρ^K)所需的副本数约为O(2^{(n-q)(K-1)})，即每投影掉一个qubit，采样成本增加因子2^{K-1}。建立了相干操作资源与额外副本数之间的精确权衡关系。
